<Review>Terrible experience. I was lied to multiple time from the start. I thought this would be the perfect place to work on my project when I saw it on group but it was absolutely useless. First off, you don't get "full access" to the workshop as listed in the benefits on groupon. In fact, you are restricted to essentially just the 3d printer unless you're willing to fork over ~$700 per type of tool and 1-2 months of your time. Doesn't matter if you've already completed wood working classes/welding etc and have proof.

This is in addition to the already high $200 monthly auto renewing fee (most cost $50-$100) which by the way, if you don't cancel exactly 10 days before auto renewal by writing to an address that's hard to find on their site, you'll continue to be charged (according to the receptionist). Turns out this was another lie because when I pressed her to allow me to cancel auto renewal since this wasn't what I expected, I could do it before the exact 10 day mark. What insanity is this?

So, when I saw the workshop wouldn't suit my needs I thought no harm no foul, maybe it works for some people. I'll just stop the sign up process and use my groupon for something else. This is where I was lied to, once again, where she said I couldn't return my groupon for credit. This is before I had even signed up mind you. When I got home I looked this up and confirmed this was another bold faced law. I would avoid this place unless you really need all of the tools and have a business use for it that is profitable because this particular location was boreline fraudulent.< /Review><gmapID>0x80dcdeb94d78de31:0x689f1db8931967ef</gmapID>< Rate>

<gmapID>0x80dcdeb94d78de31:0x689f1db8931967ef<//gmapID>< Text>
The Urban Workshop (UW) in beautiful Costa Mesa is an amazing taste of the future which is made available for you in the frame we call now! This amazing place is packed with every possible tool you will need to create the special "it"..  the it that used to be only dreams in your head... that used to be blurry wishes that you could do it... that used to be something that eventually you would see that yet another fantastic idea you had was in fact, in all actuality fantastic; yes someone did create it, they actually did get it to market... and now everyone in the world is using it.

Urban Workshop is the place to take your amazing dreams and make them; right now, today... yes I said now... it's like magic! Wrap up almost all the technologies created since the industrial revolution, put them under one roof and magically make them available, usable to everyone, to anyone... especially to you and to me. That's what I am talking about. You become the expert!

The action plan (put together by Steve, the owner of Urban Workshop) is an easy entry thing! You simply start off by joining as a member of the Urban Workshop for an amazingly low fee (the fee can be worked out to monthly, yearly or even longer). As an Urban Workshop member you now have potential super powers (you never knew most of which were even available)! You now  have access to all the super fantastic machines of industry, the very very special tools of craft and trade, the powerful computers and phenomenal applications; this is the space to spread your imaginary wings and fly into so much more...

To get you up and flying Urban offers quick intro lessons; once you are familiarized with the equipment, the tools, the process, you can start making your very own "Make" project. Your very own Dream project...

Oh!, no need to be intimidated by all of this technology. If you would like some support on getting up to flying speed there are a lot of experts at UW that are willing to help you. You may find a collaborator onsite...

Additionally, users can run there own small business right here on the premises... There are a couple of businesses successfully doing just that...

Storage space is available if you need it. That way you can have your supplies and special tools onsite...

A tour of Urban Workshop was given by Katelin, it was amazing, fun, informative and personal. Katelin introduced me to almost everything Urban is about and to top it off, she introduced me to Stephen (the owner). He was very helpful, easy to talk with despite he has so much of the Urban Workshop buzzing all around...

I had a fun time at Urban Workshop. I hope to join soon...

By:
cmilton111
Google Guide
5.17.2018< /Text>

< Review>
Urban Workshop is one of the best places to get access to industry-grade tools and systems for commercial or personal use.

Paying for a membership to Urban Workshop gives you access to a wide variety of tools and classes for you to choose from.  Machines such as Laser Engravers, Mig Welding Torches, CNC, and various others are available to you upon completing a single safety class to become familiar with the machine (the only exception to this is the CNC machine, which requires a few more classes due to its complexity).

I would strongly recommend checking out Urban Workshop if you or your child are interested in learning more about the manufacturing process.</Review>

<Text>If you are looking to use urban workshop to make a living i suggest you move on.  They do not like ambitious people there. The only people who are making money there are Steven and his buddy Troy. All they care about is class sales. You have to reserve time on a schedule to get 2 hours a week of CNC machine time. As i write this review the one and only CNC machine in the shop has been down for 5 days now. Parts ordered from china without expedite so minimum 10 days to arrive.<//Text><Pics>None</Pics>< resp>
{'time': 1518381638378, 'text': "Hi Jim,\n\nI am sorry to hear your experience with Urban Workshop did not work out the way you had hoped. We are set up as a prototyping and hobby shop so by design we are not setup for production. We have to be considerate of all of our members (over 1350 currently) who pay for and expect the same access to machinery. The access policy is not exactly as you described. Members can make reservations for 2 hour blocks on any piece of equipment and if no is waiting they can continue to use it all day long or until someone else requests access or has another reservation period.\nThe sign off classes are necessary to prevent injuries and minimize improper use of the equipment. Our desire is to allow people to get to work in the shop as quickly as possible without tying them up in classes. Most of our classes (all of them except for the CNC's) are one-time classes for no more then three hours. Students are then signed off for life. We believe this to be a very fair and reasonable arrangement that allows members to learn how the equipment operates, our community expectations, and increase safety. Please keep in mind we do need to cover teacher and material costs for classes and that on average our class prices hover around $80 per student. We believe this to be very fair for the instruction and safety it provides. The cost of other local training options are much more expensive and longer in duration, for example community colleges provide semester long programs that cost hundreds or thousands of dollars.\nWith regard to the CNC router being down this week. It is unfortunate but it happens and we are sorry if it impacted you in a negative way. We have hundreds of members of varying skill levels using all of the machines and sometimes they accidentally break things. We also have hundreds of thousands of dollars of equipment in the facility and for a small business it is impossible to stock every possible replacement part. We ordered a replacement CNC router head within 3 hours after the failure and unfortunately it is shipping from overseas. If we could get it locally we would have, but it is simply outside of our control. In this case, since the machine is one of the more popular items in the shop we will stock a spare milling head in the future to minimize member impact.\nWe apologize for any inconvenience you may have experienced and welcome you try us again in the future when you have another project to complete."}</resp>
